\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Encapsulates all the communication with a particular instance of a given rendering backend. Tries to guarantee that redundant state-\/change requests are not issued (hence "{}state guardian"{}).

There will be one of these objects for each different graphics context active in the system. 

\doxysubsection{Member Function Documentation}
\Hypertarget{classGraphicsStateGuardian_aff7472cdc5173612b2a765a07f02386d}\label{classGraphicsStateGuardian_aff7472cdc5173612b2a765a07f02386d} 
\index{GraphicsStateGuardian@{GraphicsStateGuardian}!async\_reload\_texture@{async\_reload\_texture}}
\index{async\_reload\_texture@{async\_reload\_texture}!GraphicsStateGuardian@{GraphicsStateGuardian}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{async\_reload\_texture()}{async\_reload\_texture()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classAsyncFuture}{Async\+Future}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Graphics\+State\+Guardian\+::async\+\_\+reload\+\_\+texture (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classTextureContext}{Texture\+Context}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{tc }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}

Should be called when a texture is encountered that needs to have its RAM image reloaded, and get\+\_\+incomplete\+\_\+render() is true. This will fire off a thread on the current \doxylink{classLoader}{Loader} object that will request the texture to load its image. The image will be available at some point in the future. \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
a future object that can be used to check its status. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\Hypertarget{classGraphicsStateGuardian_a57e460c01287808ca59cb976d3918d48}\label{classGraphicsStateGuardian_a57e460c01287808ca59cb976d3918d48} 
\index{GraphicsStateGuardian@{GraphicsStateGuardian}!begin\_bind\_clip\_planes@{begin\_bind\_clip\_planes}}
\index{begin\_bind\_clip\_planes@{begin\_bind\_clip\_planes}!GraphicsStateGuardian@{GraphicsStateGuardian}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{begin\_bind\_clip\_planes()}{begin\_bind\_clip\_planes()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Graphics\+State\+Guardian\+::begin\+\_\+bind\+\_\+clip\+\_\+planes (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Called immediately before \doxylink{classGraphicsStateGuardian_a13e6e0be9de80bb1ff4c3eec2d97b073}{bind\+\_\+clip\+\_\+plane()} is called, this is intended to provide the derived class a hook in which to set up some state (like transform) that might apply to several planes.

The sequence is\+: \doxylink{classGraphicsStateGuardian_a57e460c01287808ca59cb976d3918d48}{begin\+\_\+bind\+\_\+clip\+\_\+planes()} will be called, then one or more \doxylink{classGraphicsStateGuardian_a13e6e0be9de80bb1ff4c3eec2d97b073}{bind\+\_\+clip\+\_\+plane()} calls, then \doxylink{classGraphicsStateGuardian_aafe6cf78edd03722141c4d258de8a761}{end\+\_\+bind\+\_\+clip\+\_\+planes()}. \Hypertarget{classGraphicsStateGuardian_ad610c1b6e2d52a9da4fdecdefc8ca8c9}\label{classGraphicsStateGuardian_ad610c1b6e2d52a9da4fdecdefc8ca8c9} 
\index{GraphicsStateGuardian@{GraphicsStateGuardian}!begin\_bind\_lights@{begin\_bind\_lights}}
\index{begin\_bind\_lights@{begin\_bind\_lights}!GraphicsStateGuardian@{GraphicsStateGuardian}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{begin\_bind\_lights()}{begin\_bind\_lights()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Graphics\+State\+Guardian\+::begin\+\_\+bind\+\_\+lights (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Called immediately before \doxylink{classGraphicsStateGuardian_a3cb9f6ee3e5efd69881f5333749ea7f4}{bind\+\_\+light()} is called, this is intended to provide the derived class a hook in which to set up some state (like transform) that might apply to several lights.

The sequence is\+: \doxylink{classGraphicsStateGuardian_ad610c1b6e2d52a9da4fdecdefc8ca8c9}{begin\+\_\+bind\+\_\+lights()} will be called, then one or more \doxylink{classGraphicsStateGuardian_a3cb9f6ee3e5efd69881f5333749ea7f4}{bind\+\_\+light()} calls, then \doxylink{classGraphicsStateGuardian_a9a4fb424e2ea048aeca52945782879ab}{end\+\_\+bind\+\_\+lights()}. \Hypertarget{classGraphicsStateGuardian_ad878adb93c40352f545d8d95dac0095b}\label{classGraphicsStateGuardian_ad878adb93c40352f545d8d95dac0095b} 
\index{GraphicsStateGuardian@{GraphicsStateGuardian}!begin\_draw\_primitives@{begin\_draw\_primitives}}
\index{begin\_draw\_primitives@{begin\_draw\_primitives}!GraphicsStateGuardian@{GraphicsStateGuardian}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{begin\_draw\_primitives()}{begin\_draw\_primitives()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool Graphics\+State\+Guardian\+::begin\+\_\+draw\+\_\+primitives (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classGeomPipelineReader}{Geom\+Pipeline\+Reader}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{geom\+\_\+reader,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classGeomVertexDataPipelineReader}{Geom\+Vertex\+Data\+Pipeline\+Reader}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{data\+\_\+reader,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{num\+\_\+instances,  }\item[{bool}]{force }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Called before a sequence of draw\+\_\+primitive() functions are called, this should prepare the vertex data for rendering. It returns true if the vertices are ok, false to abort this group of primitives. 

Implements \mbox{\hyperlink{classGraphicsStateGuardianBase}{Graphics\+State\+Guardian\+Base}}.



Reimplemented in \mbox{\hyperlink{classDXGraphicsStateGuardian9_a8c7c04ef6dc5b0058d1fa31c59d25325}{DXGraphics\+State\+Guardian9}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{classTinyGraphicsStateGuardian_aa16e092bea5cd37b1ce58059530da1e1}{Tiny\+Graphics\+State\+Guardian}}.

\Hypertarget{classGraphicsStateGuardian_ae76699ce050f1a2ffbda6ee0ec2bdcfd}\label{classGraphicsStateGuardian_ae76699ce050f1a2ffbda6ee0ec2bdcfd} 
\index{GraphicsStateGuardian@{GraphicsStateGuardian}!begin\_frame@{begin\_frame}}
\index{begin\_frame@{begin\_frame}!GraphicsStateGuardian@{GraphicsStateGuardian}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{begin\_frame()}{begin\_frame()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool Graphics\+State\+Guardian\+::begin\+\_\+frame (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classThread}{Thread}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{current\+\_\+thread }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Called before each frame is rendered, to allow the GSG a chance to do any internal cleanup before beginning the frame.

The return value is true if successful (in which case the frame will be drawn and \doxylink{classGraphicsStateGuardian_aabb3c4bf7c00f08f1b1a4c1d570c0370}{end\+\_\+frame()} will be called later), or false if unsuccessful (in which case nothing will be drawn and \doxylink{classGraphicsStateGuardian_aabb3c4bf7c00f08f1b1a4c1d570c0370}{end\+\_\+frame()} will not be called). 

Reimplemented in \mbox{\hyperlink{classDXGraphicsStateGuardian9_a054721cda6a6d79d0085b54cc17cfaa0}{DXGraphics\+State\+Guardian9}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{classTinyGraphicsStateGuardian_a036d30b56a15d6be1b278a335d9252c5}{Tiny\+Graphics\+State\+Guardian}}.

\Hypertarget{classGraphicsStateGuardian_ac9753e06a57b00ccbfc958bdb3af75e5}\label{classGraphicsStateGuardian_ac9753e06a57b00ccbfc958bdb3af75e5} 
\index{GraphicsStateGuardian@{GraphicsStateGuardian}!begin\_occlusion\_query@{begin\_occlusion\_query}}
\index{begin\_occlusion\_query@{begin\_occlusion\_query}!GraphicsStateGuardian@{GraphicsStateGuardian}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{begin\_occlusion\_query()}{begin\_occlusion\_query()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Graphics\+State\+Guardian\+::begin\+\_\+occlusion\+\_\+query (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Begins a new occlusion query. After this call, you may call \doxylink{classGraphicsStateGuardian_ad878adb93c40352f545d8d95dac0095b}{begin\+\_\+draw\+\_\+primitives()} and \doxylink{classGraphicsStateGuardian_a348d70f85be387aae0c6ff0750d7724d}{draw\+\_\+triangles()}/draw\+\_\+whatever() repeatedly. Eventually, you should call end\+\_\+occlusion\+\_\+query() before the end of the frame; that will return a new \doxylink{classOcclusionQueryContext}{Occlusion\+Query\+Context} object that will tell you how many pixels represented by the bracketed geometry passed the depth test.

It is not valid to call \doxylink{classGraphicsStateGuardian_ac9753e06a57b00ccbfc958bdb3af75e5}{begin\+\_\+occlusion\+\_\+query()} between another \doxylink{classGraphicsStateGuardian_ac9753e06a57b00ccbfc958bdb3af75e5}{begin\+\_\+occlusion\+\_\+query()} .. end\+\_\+occlusion\+\_\+query() sequence. 

Reimplemented in \mbox{\hyperlink{classDXGraphicsStateGuardian9_ab2bba645465e8b7440349f76406c5bbf}{DXGraphics\+State\+Guardian9}}.

\Hypertarget{classGraphicsStateGuardian_a13e6e0be9de80bb1ff4c3eec2d97b073}\label{classGraphicsStateGuardian_a13e6e0be9de80bb1ff4c3eec2d97b073}

Called the first time a particular clipping plane has been bound to a given id within a frame, this should set up the associated hardware (or API) clipping plane with the plane\textquotesingle{}s properties.

Clears the framebuffer within the current \doxylink{classDisplayRegion}{Display\+Region}, according to the flags indicated by the given \doxylink{classDrawableRegion}{Drawable\+Region} object.

This does not set the \doxylink{classDisplayRegion}{Display\+Region} first. You should call \doxylink{classGraphicsStateGuardian_a60bb06c5987b92bc39591d4a27bea4ab}{prepare\+\_\+display\+\_\+region()} to specify the region you wish the clear operation to apply to.

\Hypertarget{classGraphicsStateGuardian_a7a1b237120ce4ce81e325c893a8aa6b6}\label{classGraphicsStateGuardian_a7a1b237120ce4ce81e325c893a8aa6b6} 
\index{GraphicsStateGuardian@{GraphicsStateGuardian}!do\_issue\_color@{do\_issue\_color}}
\index{do\_issue\_color@{do\_issue\_color}!GraphicsStateGuardian@{GraphicsStateGuardian}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{do\_issue\_color()}{do\_issue\_color()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Graphics\+State\+Guardian\+::do\+\_\+issue\+\_\+color (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

This method is defined in the base class because it is likely that this functionality will be used for all (or at least most) kinds of Graphics\+State\+Guardians--it\textquotesingle{}s not specific to any one rendering backend.

The Color\+Attribute just changes the interpretation of the color on the vertices, and fiddles with \+\_\+vertex\+\_\+colors\+\_\+enabled, etc. \Hypertarget{classGraphicsStateGuardian_a6b9a0eed607fa942d9177247938466e6}\label{classGraphicsStateGuardian_a6b9a0eed607fa942d9177247938466e6} 
\index{GraphicsStateGuardian@{GraphicsStateGuardian}!do\_issue\_light@{do\_issue\_light}}
\index{do\_issue\_light@{do\_issue\_light}!GraphicsStateGuardian@{GraphicsStateGuardian}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{do\_issue\_light()}{do\_issue\_light()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Graphics\+State\+Guardian\+::do\+\_\+issue\+\_\+light (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

This implementation of \doxylink{classGraphicsStateGuardian_a6b9a0eed607fa942d9177247938466e6}{do\+\_\+issue\+\_\+light()} assumes we have a limited number of hardware lights available. This function assigns each light to a different hardware light id, trying to keep each light associated with the same id where possible, but reusing id\textquotesingle{}s when necessary. When it is no longer possible to reuse existing id\textquotesingle{}s (e.\+g. all id\textquotesingle{}s are in use), the next sequential id is assigned (if available).

It will call apply\+\_\+light() each time a light is assigned to a particular id for the first time in a given frame, and it will subsequently call \doxylink{classGraphicsStateGuardian_a529d5bddc5f989a7cfb1745a4c1fecb4}{enable\+\_\+light()} to enable or disable each light as the frame is rendered, as well as \doxylink{classGraphicsStateGuardian_a902de2115281ee3cec541361a0139a37}{enable\+\_\+lighting()} to enable or disable overall lighting. 

Reimplemented in \mbox{\hyperlink{classTinyGraphicsStateGuardian_a67de428af0f815a029c735613784b7e3}{Tiny\+Graphics\+State\+Guardian}}.

\Hypertarget{classGraphicsStateGuardian_a42af326f7695741fa08f69316bb53bb3}\label{classGraphicsStateGuardian_a42af326f7695741fa08f69316bb53bb3}

\index{fetch\_specified\_part@{fetch\_specified\_part}!GraphicsStateGuardian@{GraphicsStateGuardian}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{fetch\_specified\_part()}{fetch\_specified\_part()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Graphics\+State\+Guardian\+::fetch\+\_\+specified\+\_\+part (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Shader\+::\+Shader\+Mat\+Input}]{part,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classInternalName}{Internal\+Name}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{name,  }\item[{LVec\+Base4f \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{into,  }\item[{int}]{count = {\ttfamily 1} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

See fetch\+\_\+specified\+\_\+value \Hypertarget{classGraphicsStateGuardian_a033a24fb97711cf4296c3d01cb30c8a8}\label{classGraphicsStateGuardian_a033a24fb97711cf4296c3d01cb30c8a8} 
\index{GraphicsStateGuardian@{GraphicsStateGuardian}!fetch\_specified\_value@{fetch\_specified\_value}}
\index{fetch\_specified\_value@{fetch\_specified\_value}!GraphicsStateGuardian@{GraphicsStateGuardian}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{fetch\_specified\_value()}{fetch\_specified\_value()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily const LVec\+Base4f \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Graphics\+State\+Guardian\+::fetch\+\_\+specified\+\_\+value (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structShader_1_1ShaderMatSpec}{Shader\+::\+Shader\+Mat\+Spec}} \&}]{spec,  }\item[{const LVec\+Base4f \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{cache,  }\item[{LVec\+Base4f \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{scratch }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

The gsg contains a large number of useful matrices\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item the world transform,
\item the modelview matrix,
\item the cs\+\_\+transform,
\item etc, etc.
\end{DoxyItemize}

A shader can request any of these values, and furthermore, it can request that various compositions, inverses, and transposes be performed. The Shader\+Mat\+Spec is a data structure indicating what datum is desired and what conversions to perform. This routine, fetch\+\_\+specified\+\_\+value, is responsible for doing the actual retrieval and conversions.

Some values, like the following, aren\textquotesingle{}t matrices\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item window size
\item texture coordinates of card center
\end{DoxyItemize}

This routine can fetch these values as well, by shoehorning them into a matrix. In this way, we avoid the need for a separate routine to fetch these values. \Hypertarget{classGraphicsStateGuardian_acdbe556512272fe6922f28356b43818d}\label{classGraphicsStateGuardian_acdbe556512272fe6922f28356b43818d} 
\index{GraphicsStateGuardian@{GraphicsStateGuardian}!finish\_decal@{finish\_decal}}
\index{finish\_decal@{finish\_decal}!GraphicsStateGuardian@{GraphicsStateGuardian}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{finish\_decal()}{finish\_decal()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Graphics\+State\+Guardian\+::finish\+\_\+decal (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Called during draw to clean up after decals are finished. 

Implements \mbox{\hyperlink{classGraphicsStateGuardianBase}{Graphics\+State\+Guardian\+Base}}.

\Hypertarget{classGraphicsStateGuardian_a98221f5a2c02609c1e0a72047b877018}\label{classGraphicsStateGuardian_a98221f5a2c02609c1e0a72047b877018} 
\index{GraphicsStateGuardian@{GraphicsStateGuardian}!framebuffer\_copy\_to\_ram@{framebuffer\_copy\_to\_ram}}
\index{framebuffer\_copy\_to\_ram@{framebuffer\_copy\_to\_ram}!GraphicsStateGuardian@{GraphicsStateGuardian}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{framebuffer\_copy\_to\_ram()}{framebuffer\_copy\_to\_ram()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool Graphics\+State\+Guardian\+::framebuffer\+\_\+copy\+\_\+to\+\_\+ram (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classTexture}{Texture}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{tex,  }\item[{int}]{view,  }\item[{int}]{z,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classDisplayRegion}{Display\+Region}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dr,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classRenderBuffer}{Render\+Buffer}} \&}]{rb,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classScreenshotRequest}{Screenshot\+Request}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{request = {\ttfamily nullptr} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Copy the pixels within the indicated display region from the framebuffer into system memory, not texture memory. Returns true on success, false on failure.

If a future is given, the operation may be scheduled to occur in the background, in which case the texture will be passed as the result of the future when the operation is complete.

This completely redefines the ram image of the indicated texture. 

Implements \mbox{\hyperlink{classGraphicsStateGuardianBase}{Graphics\+State\+Guardian\+Base}}.

If a \doxylink{classGeom}{Geom} needs to be rendered that requires some additional properties, the \doxylink{classStandardMunger}{Standard\+Munger} and/or the \doxylink{classCullableObject}{Cullable\+Object} will convert it as needed.

This method is declared virtual solely so that it can be queried from \doxylink{cullableObject_8cxx}{cullable\+Object.\+cxx}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool Graphics\+State\+Guardian\+::prepare\+\_\+lens (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Makes the current lens (whichever lens was most recently specified with \doxylink{classGraphicsStateGuardian_a24396aa9a8df4057bce0ddb5bbfb41dc}{set\+\_\+scene()}) active, so that it will transform future rendered geometry. Normally this is only called from the draw process, and usually it is called by \doxylink{classGraphicsStateGuardian_a24396aa9a8df4057bce0ddb5bbfb41dc}{set\+\_\+scene()}.

The return value is true if the lens is acceptable, false if it is not. 

Reimplemented in \mbox{\hyperlink{classDXGraphicsStateGuardian9_a0a229bab0d97d052a92456e5c36b5a19}{DXGraphics\+State\+Guardian9}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{classTinyGraphicsStateGuardian_a474f4ebb83cf966bd756279f4c24bac1}{Tiny\+Graphics\+State\+Guardian}}.

Creates whatever structures the GSG requires to represent the sampler internally, and returns a newly-\/allocated \doxylink{classSamplerContext}{Sampler\+Context} object with this data. \Hypertarget{classGraphicsStateGuardian_a3f9a5b16ca9cc831680f840206fe673f}\label{classGraphicsStateGuardian_a3f9a5b16ca9cc831680f840206fe673f} 
\index{GraphicsStateGuardian@{GraphicsStateGuardian}!set\_coordinate\_system@{set\_coordinate\_system}}
\index{set\_coordinate\_system@{set\_coordinate\_system}!GraphicsStateGuardian@{GraphicsStateGuardian}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{set\_coordinate\_system()}{set\_coordinate\_system()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Graphics\+State\+Guardian\+::set\+\_\+coordinate\+\_\+system (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Coordinate\+System}]{cs }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Changes the coordinate system in effect on this particular gsg. This is also called the "{}external"{} coordinate system, since it is the coordinate system used by the scene graph, external to to GSG.

Normally, this will be the default coordinate system, but it might be set differently at runtime. It will automatically be copied from the current lens\textquotesingle{}s coordinate system as each \doxylink{classDisplayRegion}{Display\+Region} is rendered. \Hypertarget{classGraphicsStateGuardian_af63bd0cb47f242381230d9036825ded5}\label{classGraphicsStateGuardian_af63bd0cb47f242381230d9036825ded5} 
\index{GraphicsStateGuardian@{GraphicsStateGuardian}!set\_flash\_texture@{set\_flash\_texture}}
\index{set\_flash\_texture@{set\_flash\_texture}!GraphicsStateGuardian@{GraphicsStateGuardian}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{set\_flash\_texture()}{set\_flash\_texture()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Graphics\+State\+Guardian\+::set\+\_\+flash\+\_\+texture (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classTexture}{Texture}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{tex }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets the "{}flash texture"{}. This is a debug feature; when enabled, the specified texture will begin flashing in the scene, helping you to find it visually.

The texture also flashes with a color code\+: blue for mipmap level 0, yellow for mipmap level 1, and red for mipmap level 2 or higher (even for textures that don\textquotesingle{}t have mipmaps). This gives you an idea of the choice of the texture size. If it is blue, the texture is being drawn the proper size or magnified; if it is yellow, it is being minified a little bit; and if it red, it is being minified considerably. If you see a red texture when you are right in front of it, you should consider reducing the size of the texture to avoid wasting texture memory.

Not all rendering backends support the flash\+\_\+texture feature. Presently, it is only supported by Open\+GL. \Hypertarget{classGraphicsStateGuardian_adef9d79dd4866cbfa7056ff939c482f9}\label{classGraphicsStateGuardian_adef9d79dd4866cbfa7056ff939c482f9} 
\index{GraphicsStateGuardian@{GraphicsStateGuardian}!set\_gamma@{set\_gamma}}
\index{set\_gamma@{set\_gamma}!GraphicsStateGuardian@{GraphicsStateGuardian}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{set\_gamma()}{set\_gamma()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool Graphics\+State\+Guardian\+::set\+\_\+gamma (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{PN\+\_\+stdfloat}]{gamma }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Set gamma. Returns true on success. 

Reimplemented in \mbox{\hyperlink{classDXGraphicsStateGuardian9_a5901ccd664c31187d7724853294bd720}{DXGraphics\+State\+Guardian9}}.

\Hypertarget{classGraphicsStateGuardian_a24396aa9a8df4057bce0ddb5bbfb41dc}\label{classGraphicsStateGuardian_a24396aa9a8df4057bce0ddb5bbfb41dc}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool Graphics\+State\+Guardian\+::set\+\_\+scene (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classSceneSetup}{Scene\+Setup}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{scene\+\_\+setup }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets the \doxylink{classSceneSetup}{Scene\+Setup} object that indicates the initial camera position, etc. This must be called before traversal begins. Returns true if the scene is acceptable, false if something\textquotesingle{}s wrong. This should be called in the draw thread only. \Hypertarget{classGraphicsStateGuardian_ad6f69fb763c86c69eca984c49c92c36a}\label{classGraphicsStateGuardian_ad6f69fb763c86c69eca984c49c92c36a} 
\index{GraphicsStateGuardian@{GraphicsStateGuardian}!set\_state\_and\_transform@{set\_state\_and\_transform}}
\index{set\_state\_and\_transform@{set\_state\_and\_transform}!GraphicsStateGuardian@{GraphicsStateGuardian}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{set\_state\_and\_transform()}{set\_state\_and\_transform()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Graphics\+State\+Guardian\+::set\+\_\+state\+\_\+and\+\_\+transform (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classRenderState}{Render\+State}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{state,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classTransformState}{Transform\+State}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{trans }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Simultaneously resets the render state and the transform state.

This transform specified is the "{}internal"{} net transform, already converted into the GSG\textquotesingle{}s internal coordinate space by composing it to get\+\_\+cs\+\_\+transform(). (Previously, this used to be the "{}external"{} net transform, with the assumption that that GSG would convert it internally, but that is no longer the case.)

Special case\+: if (state==NULL), then the target state is already stored in \+\_\+target. 

Implements \mbox{\hyperlink{classGraphicsStateGuardianBase}{Graphics\+State\+Guardian\+Base}}.



Reimplemented in \mbox{\hyperlink{classDXGraphicsStateGuardian9_aa16ad8ee5ecbcc92e7f34e109ae69566}{DXGraphics\+State\+Guardian9}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{classTinyGraphicsStateGuardian_a974a2440241ae52f0c0ec56876ea9d8f}{Tiny\+Graphics\+State\+Guardian}}.

\Hypertarget{classGraphicsStateGuardian_a496ca9580b63ec26834fa037ee0b00b9}\label{classGraphicsStateGuardian_a496ca9580b63ec26834fa037ee0b00b9} 
\index{GraphicsStateGuardian@{GraphicsStateGuardian}!traverse\_prepared\_textures@{traverse\_prepared\_textures}}
\index{traverse\_prepared\_textures@{traverse\_prepared\_textures}!GraphicsStateGuardian@{GraphicsStateGuardian}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{traverse\_prepared\_textures()}{traverse\_prepared\_textures()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Graphics\+State\+Guardian\+::traverse\+\_\+prepared\+\_\+textures (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Graphics\+State\+Guardian\+::\+Texture\+Callback \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{func,  }\item[{void \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{callback\+\_\+arg }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Calls the indicated function on all currently-\/prepared textures, or until the callback function returns false. \Hypertarget{classGraphicsStateGuardian_a3ee43e9c2ad6748f9019683de0461235}\label{classGraphicsStateGuardian_a3ee43e9c2ad6748f9019683de0461235} 
\index{GraphicsStateGuardian@{GraphicsStateGuardian}!update\_shader\_matrix\_cache@{update\_shader\_matrix\_cache}}
\index{update\_shader\_matrix\_cache@{update\_shader\_matrix\_cache}!GraphicsStateGuardian@{GraphicsStateGuardian}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{update\_shader\_matrix\_cache()}{update\_shader\_matrix\_cache()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Graphics\+State\+Guardian\+::update\+\_\+shader\+\_\+matrix\+\_\+cache (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classShader}{Shader}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{shader,  }\item[{LVec\+Base4f \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{cache,  }\item[{int}]{altered }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

A shader can request a number of values from the current render state. These are stored in the form of a matrix. Each \doxylink{classShaderContext}{Shader\+Context} caches the current value of these matrices, and calls this routine to update the matrices that have changed based on the aspects of the render state that were altered. \Hypertarget{classGraphicsStateGuardian_a2582880d4f5d1fce9dbcca2a9df49a49}\label{classGraphicsStateGuardian_a2582880d4f5d1fce9dbcca2a9df49a49} 
\index{GraphicsStateGuardian@{GraphicsStateGuardian}!update\_texture@{update\_texture}}
\index{update\_texture@{update\_texture}!GraphicsStateGuardian@{GraphicsStateGuardian}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{update\_texture()}{update\_texture()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool Graphics\+State\+Guardian\+::update\+\_\+texture (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classTextureContext}{Texture\+Context}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{tc,  }\item[{bool}]{force }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Ensures that the current \doxylink{classTexture}{Texture} data is refreshed onto the GSG. This means updating the texture properties and/or re-\/uploading the texture image, if necessary. This should only be called within the draw thread.

If force is true, this function will not return until the texture has been fully uploaded. If force is false, the function may choose to upload a simple version of the texture instead, if the texture is not fully resident (and if get\+\_\+incomplete\+\_\+render() is true). 

Implements \mbox{\hyperlink{classGraphicsStateGuardianBase}{Graphics\+State\+Guardian\+Base}}.



Reimplemented in \mbox{\hyperlink{classDXGraphicsStateGuardian9_a5360d6156eced033ef304521ba98787c}{DXGraphics\+State\+Guardian9}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{classTinyGraphicsStateGuardian_aa66b711a5920309e1196e259968fa622}{Tiny\+Graphics\+State\+Guardian}}.

\Hypertarget{classGraphicsStateGuardian_a3690ae70c039ff06279726ab8d45fad4}\label{classGraphicsStateGuardian_a3690ae70c039ff06279726ab8d45fad4}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{update\_texture()}{update\_texture()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool Graphics\+State\+Guardian\+::update\+\_\+texture (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classTextureContext}{Texture\+Context}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{tc,  }\item[{bool}]{force,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classCompletionToken}{Completion\+Token}}}]{token }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Ensures that the current \doxylink{classTexture}{Texture} data is refreshed onto the GSG. This means updating the texture properties and/or re-\/uploading the texture image, if necessary. This should only be called within the draw thread.

If force is true, this function will not return until the texture has been fully uploaded. If force is false, the function may choose to upload a simple version of the texture instead, if the texture is not fully resident (and if get\+\_\+incomplete\+\_\+render() is true).
